1515827541337< /time>
< user>
106204217155651321562</user>
<resp>None< /resp>< review>
THE SINGLE WORST HAIRCUT I HAVE EVER HAD! First off, I want to clarify that I rarely leave reviews and this is the first negative review I have ever written. I feel the need to leave this review to save others from having the same experience I have had. I sat down and was asked how I would like my hair to be cut. I happily told the lady I would like a #3 on the sides and a #7 on top, clarifying that I would like the longest hair on my head to be 3/4" long. She says okay and gets to it. We have a pleasant conversation about my recent move to the city and what part of town I live in. She starts off with the #7 comb on top, but she is going in the wrong direction with it, laying my hair down and just sliding over the top. She does this 6 or 7 times, then goes at it from a slight angle, still barely knicking the 2" or 2.5" hairs. She stops, having made hardly any difference and asks, "Shorter?" I say, "Yeah, down to three-quarters of an inch." She goes at it again in the wrong direction, acting as if she has never cut hair before. Then she switches out the comb on the clippers for a longer one, telling me that my hair "has a wave to it". This comb prevents her from cutting any hair at all, so she switches back to the first comb. Then she stop and asks again, "Is that good, or shorter still?" I tell her, "A little more. It's still pretty long." The hairs are still at least 2" long on the top of my head. She goes at it again, this time from the front and moving toward the back, making more progress, but still the hairs are longer than an inch and a half. She stops and asks again, "Shorter still?" I sort of laugh and tell her, "You can bring them down to three-quarters of an inch." I hold up my fingers to demonstrate that length. She says okay, then turns me away from the mirror for the rest of the haircut. At times during the haircut, I notice she is using the clippers with no comb at all, freestyle, holding them with both hands and making a jabbing motion at the side of my head to get the hairs. She holds up a mirror for me a few times, but points it over my head or at my chin instead of just turning me back around to see. After 40 minutes of sitting in her chair feeling like she was experimenting with all the tools available to her on her first day, she holds the mirror up for me again and asks if I like it. At first glance, in the little mirror it looks okay, so I say great. She thanks me and I go to pay. I am told at the time of check out that the credit/debit machine is broken and I can pay in cash only. The ATM in the parking lot charges me $3. I made this appointment a day in advance. A heads up on the credit problem would have been nice. I walk out and notice I am completely plastered in hair, not unusual after a haircut, but still unpleasant. Upon arriving home, I look in my bathroom mirror to discover that the left side of my hair is significantly longer than the right side. The right side is about right with .75" on top, .3 inches on the side.. But the left side is at least 1.5" on top, all the way from the midpoint on my head to the back edge of the top. I spend the next half hour in the bathroom with a pair of scissors, cutting my own hair. There were 5 or 6 inch-long hairs over each ear, hanging down, touching my ears. I eventually got the top to be more or less even. The top/back was nearly impossible to do myself, but my roommate says it looks good now. I just can't figure out what this lady was doing to my hair for 40 minutes. Maybe it was legitimately her first day, and if that is the case, then I take it all back, but that wasn't the feeling I got. She should find another gig because cutting hair is not it for her.</review>

In one word 'average'. The moment you walk in, you get an underground illegal surgery place kind of feel with all the employees wearing surgical masks and gloves. I initially had high expectations for this place. But was thoroughly disappointed by the service and quality of the food. The pork belly bun we ordered was way over cooked. We waited for 45 minutes for the rest of the dishes and then had an order mixup, then waited again. While the salmon in the salmon rice bowl we ordered was pretty flavorful and well done, the rice was coated in excessive amount of butter which made the dish overall very unappetizing.

So overall pros
Great food presentation
Well done meat

Cons
Long waiting time
Greasy food
Hectic service</review>

< Review>
Small restaurant feels very cozy. We came by once they were open at 5:30, and the restaurant was already half full. That goes to show that the restaurant is pretty popular. I love the casual atmosphere here and the nose level isn't to overbearing. The pork belly bun is definitely my favorite among all the other buns with the smoked salmon a close second. The noodle bowls are delicious, but I feel they might be lacking in something. We ordered the Pork Noodle and didn't have to wait too long for the dish. The pork and the broth was very savory, I feel like it needed something sweet to go along with it (possibly sweet daikon or something along the lines of a hoisen sauce) to cut through the strong flavors. Aside from this, I'm giving 4 stars, not just for food, but also for the service. There is only one server on hand for the whole restaurant (probably seats 30 people total) most of the time. She's very nice, but when the restaurant is full, it's hard to get her attention when you need something since she's running around. They do have a second server now so it's a bit easier to get your needs met. Aside from that, I'm definitely coming back here.<//Review>

<response>None<//response>< Review>
Surprised by how tasty the vegetarian ramen was. I liked the creamy soup more than my friend did - it was a bit too rich for her. For me, it was a good balance - I've had richer tonkotsu or torisoba so... I agree with the reviewer who thought the ramen was more Chinese-Japanese style. This is definitely a fusion place.

The brussel sprouts in the warm eggplant salad were great. The eggplant wasn't bad but the oil got a bit heavy.

The poached salmon rice bowl was average.

Next time I'd like to try the beet salad and the other noodle options.

A slight side-eye to the waitress who wouldn't seat my 2 person group at a corner 2 person table saying it wasn't clean, and later let a couple sit at a 4 person table, and then let another couple sit at the same "dirty" corner table. Someone at the 4 person table right next to me kept burping. I guess one can't help burping.< /Review>

<name>Cindy Toh< /name><time>1472427518595</time>< Rate>
5<//Rate>
<Review>Craving for Japanese Ramen or Pork Bun? Visit this place right now!

== Food ==
Pork Belly Bun (5/5)
Da bomb! Served on a fancy wooden serving board, the bun super mouth watering (presentation matters!).

True enough, it tasted so so good. The pork belly was juicy, slightly crunch and oh so yummy! The buns were superb, it was really soft and fluffy, I would like to think they made this from scratch!

Spicy Beef Ramen (5/5)
When it arrived, I thought I was in for some trouble. The redness of the soup made me think it's gonna be ultra spicy.

The first mouth I had, it was love at first mouth! The combination of the vegetable, the meat, the bouncy noodles, corn and spice that made this an amazing combo. Super super love it.

Soy Sauce Beef Rice Bowl (4/5)
Sizeable bowl, nicely spread out. Steamed vegetables on one side, beef chunk, beef slices, rice and the soy sauce on the beef.

It was a delightful and tasty meal. Even so, the two above beat this dish by miles. The next time I'm back, I'm going to try a different bun and a different noodles.

== SERVICE / AMBiENCE ==
Cozy restaurant, expect to be seated considerably close to other patrons. Might be tough for groups to get sitting and likely would have to wait for quite awhile.

Parties < 4 should be able to secure a seat decently fast. We were lucky and there were two seats available, patrons after us had to wait approx 10-15mins before they were seated. They have a name list where you would need to put your name down.

Servers were polite and prompt. Food was considerably ok speed given how busy the restaurant is.

I am in love with their food now, excited to be back for more!< /Review>< pics>

The menu was simple and the food was delicious. This place feels like a home-y yet quality restaurant.
I had the garlic noodles with the chasiu. The chasiu is not really chasiu -  more like a cross between chasiu and ribs. They were tender and not too fatty. Noodles were perfectly al dente and the flavour was really good, especially with the fried onion garnish stirred in. It did feel a bit oily and salty towards the bottom of the dish. Asparagus was amazing: nice balance between crisp and soft.<//Text>

<Date>1507082919510</Date><rate>4< /rate>< review>
Nice park along the Sacramento River, but more for leisurely walking and bike riding. Beautiful views of Old Sacramento and downtown Sacramento. The bathrooms loom scary since a lot of homesless people use them, and a lot of transients tend to hang out along this park. Definitely worth checking oir the annual West Sacramento Cyclocross Grand Prix in Oct. Every year. Fun event at this park.</review>

West Sac is an up-and-coming area and there will be more and more to do. Burgers and Brew is just a few blocks away in the historical Old Firehouse.
